style by Ken Traub Olin Shivers82 also using elements of esub2acm cls83 LATEST REVISION V2 6SP OCTOBER 2 284 ARTICLE DOCUMENT STYLE Released 16 March 198885 for LaTeX version 2 986 Copyright C 1988 by Leslie Lamport87 88 89 ACM PROC ARTICLE SP is a document style for producing two column camera ready pages for9 ACM conferences according to ACM specifications The main features of91 this style are 92 93 1 Two columns 94 2 Side and top margins of 4 5pc bottom margin of 6pc column gutter of95 2pc hence columns are 2 pc wide and 55 5pc tall 6pc 3D 1in approx 96 3 First page has title information and an extra 6pc of space at the97 bottom of the first column for the ACM copyright notice 98 4 Text is 9pt on 1 pt baselines titles except main are 9pt bold 99 1 1 1 There are a few restrictions you must observe 1 2 1 3 1 You cannot change the font size ACM wants you to use 9pt 1 4 3 You must start your paper with the maketitle command Prior to the1 5 maketitle you must have title and author commands If you have a1 6 date command it will be ignored no date appears on the paper since1 7 the proceedings will have a date on the front cover 1 8 4 Marginal paragraphs tables of contents lists of figures and tables 1 9 and page headings are all forbidden 11 5 The figure environment will produce a figure one column wide if you111 want one that is two columns wide use figure 112 113 114 Copyright Space 115 This style automatically leaves 1 blank space at the bottom of page 1 116 column 1 This space can optionally be filled with some text using the117 toappear command If used this command must be BEFORE the maketitle118 command If this command is defined AND preprint is on then the119 space is filled with the text at the bottom otherwise it is12 blank If you use toappearbox instead of toappear then a121 box will be drawn around the text if preprint is on 122 123 A typical usage looks like this 124 toappear To appear in the Ninth AES Conference on Medievil Lithuanian125 Embalming Technique June 1991 Alfaretta Georgia 126 This will be included in the preprint and left out of the conference127 version 128 129 WARNING 13 Some dvi ps converters heuristically allow chars to drift from their131 true positions a few pixels This may be noticeable with the 9pt sans serif132 bold font used for section headers 133 You may turn this hackery off via the e option 134 dvips e foo dvi foo
